***просивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:просивший.html>проси́вший</a> (349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">просид(е́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prosid(étʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> [<a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> → <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и́</a>; д → <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a>] + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for some time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, to sit up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for some time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, to spend one's time in a sitting position, to spend one's time under confinement, to stay <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for some time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***просить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>проси́ть</a> (349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prositi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*preḱ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pray</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">precarious</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>to ask

<li>to long <i>(for)</i>, to yearn <i>(for)</i>, to thirst <i>(for)</i>

***просиять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:просиять.html>просия́ть</a> (15646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиять.html>сия́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sijátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просиять.html>просия́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prosijátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><i>(sun)</i> to come out, to begin to shine, to shine</li>
<li>to brighten <i>(with)</i>, to light up <i>(with)</i>, to beam <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:просиять.html>просия́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prosijátʹ</b> ot rádosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beam with joy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:просиять.html>просия́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jejó licó <b>prosijálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">her face lit up</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***проскакивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проскакивать.html>проска́кивать</a> (21260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проскок-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proskok-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскакивать.html>проска́кивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proskákivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush, to dart, to dash, to fly, to shoot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:электрод.html>электро́дами</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскакивать.html>проска́кивали</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:искра.html>и́скры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méždu elektródami <b>proskákivali</b> ískry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sparks shot between the electrodes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go <i>(past)</i>, to leave <i>(behind)</i>, to cross, to make it <i>(across)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss, to overshoot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall <i>(through, between)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip in, to sneak in, to slip <i>(into)</i>, to sneak <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manage to become <i>(smb)</i>, to manage to get <i>(somewhere)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make it <i>(through)</i>, to manage, to cope <i>(with)</i>, to hurdle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскакивать.html>проска́кивают</a></b> диале́ктные <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jevó réči <b>proskákivajut</b> dialéktnyje slová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dialect words slip out now and then in his speech</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip by, to pass quickly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">rush, dart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мчаться.html>мча́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mčátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">miss</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропускать.html>пропуска́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">propuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проскальзывать.html>проска́льзывать</a> (19362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскользнуть.html>проскользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proskolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскальзывать.html>проска́льзывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proskálʹzyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскользнуть.html>проскользну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to steal, to sneak, to slip</li>
<li>to slip out, to be discernible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскальзывать.html>проска́льзывают</a></b> диале́ктные <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jevó réči <b>proskálʹzyvajut</b> dialéktnyje slova</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dialect words slip out now and then in his speech</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́нии</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскальзывать.html>проска́льзывает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ирония.html>иро́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jejó soobščénii <b>proskálʹzyvajet</b> irónija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a touch of irony in her report</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проскользнуть.html>проскользну́вший</a> (12661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскользнуть.html>проскользну́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proskolʹznúvšij</span>)

***проскользнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проскользнуть.html>проскользну́ть</a> (12661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскользнуть.html>проскользну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proskolʹznútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскальзывать.html>проска́льзывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to steal, to sneak, to slip</li>
<li>to slip out, to be discernible</li></ol>

***проскочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a> (6763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">скочи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proskočítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскакивать.html>проска́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush, to dart, to dash, to fly, to shoot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go <i>(past)</i>, to leave <i>(behind)</i>, to cross, to make it <i>(across)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекресток.html>перекрёсток</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašína jedvá <b>proskočíla</b> perekrjóstok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the car just barely crossed the intersection</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss, to overshoot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остановка.html>остано́вку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proskočítʹ</b> svojú ostanóvku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to miss one's stop</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поворот.html>поворо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:магистраль.html>магистра́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proskočítʹ</b> povorót s magistráli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to miss/overshoot the exit from the highway</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall <i>(through, between)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip in, to sneak in, to slip <i>(into)</i>, to sneak <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manage to become <i>(smb)</i>, to manage to get <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальник.html>нача́льники</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proskočítʹ</b> v načálʹniki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to manage to become a boss</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:университет.html>университе́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proskočítʹ</b> v universitét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to manage to enter the university</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дамка.html>да́мки</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шке</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proskočítʹ</b> v dámki (o šáške)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to manage to get crowned</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make it <i>(through)</i>, to manage, to cope <i>(with)</i>, to hurdle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́л</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sam ne znáju, kak ja <b>proskočíl</b> (čérez) ekzámen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't know myself how I made it through the exam</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:информация.html>информа́ция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могла́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пресса.html>пре́ссу</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak éta informácija moglá <b>proskočítʹ</b> v préssu?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how could this information have leaked [slipped out] into the press?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proskočílo</b> mnógo ošíbok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">many errors have crept / slipped in</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slip by, to pass quickly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проскочить.html>проскочи́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:незаметно.html>незаме́тно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">léto <b>proskočílo</b> nezamétno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the summer slipped by before we [they, etc] knew it</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">rush, dart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промчаться.html>промча́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">promčátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***прославить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прославить.html>просла́вить</a> (6633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:славить.html>сла́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прославить.html>просла́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proslávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прославлять.html>прославля́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">просла́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to glorify, to sing the praises of</li>
<li>to make famous</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander, to defame</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прославить.html>просла́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proslávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прославиться.html>просла́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proslávitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прославля́ться</b>)

<ol><li>to become famous <i>(for)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become notorious <i>(for)</i></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прославить.html>просла́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proslávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***проследить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>проследи́ть</a> (6477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следить.html>следи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sledítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>проследи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prosledítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прослеживать.html>просле́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spy <i>(on)</i>, to track</li>
<li>to trail, to follow</li>
<li>to trace, to retrace <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to track the development of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to observe, to see to (it), to make sure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>проследи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выполнение.html>выполне́нием</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prosledítʹ</b> za vypolnénijem čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make sure something gets done</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>прослежу́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> ...</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>prosležú</b> za étim, štóby ...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll see to it that ...</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проследовать.html>просле́довать</a> (12864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slédovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***прослеживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прослеживать.html>просле́живать</a> (28401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>проследи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prosledítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прослеживать.html>просле́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prosléživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проследить.html>проследи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spy <i>(on)</i>, to track</li>
<li>to trail, to follow</li>
<li>to trace, to retrace <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to track the development of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to observe, to see to (it), to make sure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прослеживать.html>просле́живать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выполнение.html>выполне́нием</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prosléživatʹ</b> za vypolnénijem čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make sure something gets done</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прослеживать.html>просле́живать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> ...</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prosléživatʹ</b> za étim, štóby ...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to see to it that ...</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прослеживаться.html>просле́живаться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prosléživatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проследи́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prosledítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
